{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Real\+Type $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecompnal_a7d6082c366cc92ba48d14a1f91c7e223}{Map}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecompnal_a79aaace56ee99c030c6feafd025fd651}{Vec\+Int\+Pair}}, std\+::vector$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecompnal_a5c65468895022d33488c22744a8c46fc}{LInt}}$>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structcompnal_1_1_vec_int_hash}{Vec\+Int\+Hash}}$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcompnal_1_1model_1_1_base_u1_spin_multi_electrons__1_d}{compnal\+::model\+::\+Base\+U1\+Spin\+Multi\+Electrons\+\_\+1D}}$<$ Real\+Type $>$\+::bases\+\_\+\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}



Bases of the target Hilbert space specified by the system size $ N$, the magnitude of the local spin $ S$, the number of the total electrons at each orbital $ \langle\hat{N}_{{\rm e}, \alpha}\rangle$, and the total sz $ \langle\hat{S}^{z}_{\rm tot}\rangle $. The first value of std\+::vector$<$int$>$ stores twice the number of the total sz and remaining values correspond to the orbitals of the electrons.
